<div id="review_462060825" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/462060825" />
    <a title="Danielle (Danniegurl)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/10879719-danielle-danniegurl"><img alt="Danielle (Danniegurl)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1514066931p2/10879719.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/462060825?book_show_action=true">Mar 20, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Danielle (Danniegurl)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Danielle (Danniegurl)" href="/user/show/10879719-danielle-danniegurl">Danielle (Danniegurl)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10879719-danielle-danniegurl?shelf=magic-witches-etc-read">magic-witches-etc-read</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10879719-danielle-danniegurl?shelf=paranormal-romance-read">paranormal-romance-read</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10879719-danielle-danniegurl?shelf=4-stars">4-stars</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10879719-danielle-danniegurl?shelf=i-see-dead-people">i-see-dead-people</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10879719-danielle-danniegurl?shelf=faeries">faeries</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10879719-danielle-danniegurl?shelf=paranormal-ya">paranormal-ya</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10879719-danielle-danniegurl?shelf=ghosts-and-such">ghosts-and-such</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10879719-danielle-danniegurl?shelf=pov-one">pov-one</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer462060825" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1823830104413695927">So I thought I was going to have a problem with this one because I've not really been able to get into YA lately. YA is just boring and the angst is wahhh. But I was pleasantly surprised with this book. The writing in this book was well written enough for me to immediately sink my teeth into it. The story itself was fast paced enough to gain my interest AND keep it. So in this book Kaylee was locked up for her "psychotic" break down in a mall where she couldn't stop screaming and kept screaming </span>
  <span id="freeText1823830104413695927" style="display:none">So I thought I was going to have a problem with this one because I've not really been able to get into YA lately. YA is just boring and the angst is wahhh. But I was pleasantly surprised with this book. The writing in this book was well written enough for me to immediately sink my teeth into it. The story itself was fast paced enough to gain my interest AND keep it. So in this book Kaylee was locked up for her "psychotic" break down in a mall where she couldn't stop screaming and kept screaming for an hour. Later after she sneaks out of her house to go to a club the "panic attacks" happen again. She has to clamp her mouth shut to not let the scream out. Nash, a sorta hunky popular guy from school, is there and was talking to her before this incident. When it becomes apparent that Kaylee is having an issue the only one who can help her is Nash. Surprisingly Nash doesn't think that Kaylee is crazy and takes some interest in her. Then another girl a few days later drops dead and Kaylee doesn't think she was "supposed" to die. Thus begins the adventure that Kaylee and Nash find themselves in.<br /><br />The book is fascinating in a world where there are banshees (<i>bean sidhe</i> is actually how it's written but my brain kept trying to self correct) and grim reapers and such we still don't know the full extent of the world. <br /><br />In some ways I feel like we just scratched the surface about this world with bean sidhe, but in others I felt kind of lost. When the culprit is revealed I was surprised, and not exactly shocked by wondering WHY the person did what they did. And that doesn't become too clear. There is a motive, but I don't understand what was actually supposed to happen. Anyways the story leaves some holes although in the beginning the author's dedication said something about something filling plot holes so perhaps she is aware of them in this book and is going to fill them in later down the road. I sure hope so. The perimeters still aren't concrete enough for me to exactly know what is going on here.<br /><br />As for the romance with Nash and Kaylee I have a feeling there is some fated mate stuff going on here though it wasn't mentioned, it felt implied. I don't know how I feel about it, but I also feel like there is a possibility for there to be a love triangle too. Who knows. I sure don't. <br /><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="1823830104413695927" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_270911637" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/270911637" />
    <a title="Sarah Elizabeth" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/7591340-sarah-elizabeth"><img alt="Sarah Elizabeth" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1328957304p2/7591340.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/270911637?book_show_action=true">Feb 01, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Sarah Elizabeth" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Sarah Elizabeth" href="/user/show/7591340-sarah-elizabeth">Sarah Elizabeth</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7591340-sarah-elizabeth?shelf=as">as</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7591340-sarah-elizabeth?shelf=gift">gift</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7591340-sarah-elizabeth?shelf=read-2013">read-2013</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer270911637" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12417697444107653162">(Source: I own a copy of this book.)<br/>16-year-old Kaylee has a secret, she knows when someone close by is going to die, and has this irrepressible urge to scream at the top of her lungs.<br/>This wouldn’t usually be too much of a problem, but suddenly teen girls are dropping down dead for no obvious reason, and Kaylee knows that her aunt and uncle are keeping something secret from her – something about her and her life.<br/>Who is killing these girls? Why does Kaylee feel the need to scream when someone is </span>
  <span id="freeText12417697444107653162" style="display:none">(Source: I own a copy of this book.)<br />16-year-old Kaylee has a secret, she knows when someone close by is going to die, and has this irrepressible urge to scream at the top of her lungs.<br />This wouldn’t usually be too much of a problem, but suddenly teen girls are dropping down dead for no obvious reason, and Kaylee knows that her aunt and uncle are keeping something secret from her – something about her and her life.<br />Who is killing these girls? Why does Kaylee feel the need to scream when someone is about to die? And what life-changing secret are her aunt and uncle hiding from her?<br /><br /><br />This was a great YA paranormal story and I have to say that I don’t think I’ve read anything quite like this before.<br /><br />Kaylee was a strong lead character, and I liked the way that she stood up and took charge of the situation when it was needed. I felt really bad for her at first – imagine screaming at the top of your lungs and being unable to stop it! When I found out what Kaylee was really about though I was surprised – I can’t say that I’ve read any other books with this kind of paranormal ability, and it was quite a refreshing change.<br /><br />I liked Nash (the love interest), although I didn’t love him. While I thought that Kaylee and Nash were cute together, and that they made a sweet couple, there wasn’t the kind of heart-beating-fast romance that you sometimes find in these sort of books.<br /><br />I liked the storyline in this book and the little twists and turns and unpredictability. I totally didn’t guess what was going on, and I didn’t guess who was ultimately to blame either. I liked the mystery of who killed the girls, as well as the mystery of what Kaylee was really about. I can’t imagine where the next book will go from here but I’m really interested to find out!<br />Overall; a different kind of paranormal YA story.<br />8 out of 10.<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="12417697444107653162" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('EEDWXjNs2wdjsg1mDWOzzKxVWN9j3uoGlL+N81vwCO21b50CgigT5L58Bm5ROIcgEXJ+2r5wq9TsxSQCLOR4AA==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('5QuKQ2bsuUVZz6ovVnDdKormsay0MWXtQPHKsVqOSj5AJMEf16hxpoQBoScKK+nGN8GXqWmfJD84i2NALZo60w==')})
  }
